FNV GRAPHICS FOG/WEATHER DEEP FIELD AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which real code references fog/weather/climate strings or settings?
2. Which functions read or write TESWeather fog near/far/color fields?
3. Which Sky/TES fields are current weather, next weather, and transition percent?
4. Can Psycho read fog constants safely before ProcessImageSpaceShaders?
